Story of both cassanova and gangster. ^__^ magiging happy ending kaya sila? Si  Abigail Barbie Cruz ay Gorgeous, hot, sexy, rich, kind, ma-appeal genius and friendly but she's a gangster not just an ordinary gangster because she's the Queen of the GANGSTER!  Master niya lahat ng sports especially tennis, martial arts, gun, stick, and sword. She become a playgirl because of her fucking bastard ex- boyfriend!! Then she met Ken Stephen Castro Handsome, hot (six packs haha), rich, genius, spoiled brat,  suplado, ma-appeal, short-tempered and His a gang leader not just an ordinary gang leader because his the King of the GANGSTER.
 Rank 1 ang gang niya sa pilipinas. Master niya lahat ng sports especially tennis, martial arts, gun, stick, and sword. Hindi siya naniniwala sa LOVE but when she met Abigail naniwala na siya sa love pero pa'no kung hindi mainlove si Abigail sa kanya dahil sa past ni Abigail? Anong mangyayari sa kanila? Just read my story!

(A/N: A volley in tennis is a shot in which the ball is struck before it bounces on the ground. 

 

backspin (also known as slice or underspin), is a shot such that the ball rotates backwards (as though rolling back towards the player) after it is hit.

 

 A lob in tennis is hitting the ball high and deep into the opponent's court.

 

 A smash in tennis is a shot that is hit above the head with a serve-like motion)
